| | | | |
|:---:|:------------:|:---------:|:---------:|
| 1\. | **चखान–चखन** | **चख्निव** | **चख्निम** |
| 2\. | **चखनिथ** | **चख्नथुः** | **चख्न** |
| 3\. | **चखान** | **चख्नतुः** | **चख्नुः** |

** ***Atmanepada.*

| | | | |
|:---:|:---------:|:----------:|:----------:|
| 1\. | **चख्ने** | **चख्निवहे** | **चख्निमहे** |
| 2\. | **चख्निषे** | **चख्नाथे** | **चख्निध्वे** |
| 3\. | **चख्ने** | **चख्नाते** | **चख्निरे** |

For **घस्** see under 195.

 (200) [When](https://#%C2%A0 "इग्यणः सम्प्रसारणम्। 1. 1. 45. न सम्प्रसारणे सम्प्रसारणम्। 6. 1. 37. सम्प्रसारणाच्च। 6.1.108.") **य्, व्, र्, ल्,** are changed to **इ, उ, ऋ, लृ** respectively, the vowel so substituted is called Samprasâraṇa.** **

 When both the members of a conjunct consonant admit of Samprasâraṇa, the second semi-vowel only takes it.

 If a Samprasâraṇa is followed by another vowel, the Samprasâraṇa is substituted for both.

 Before the weak terminations of the Perfect, Samprasâraṇa takes place both in the reduplicative syllable and the semi-vowel of the root, but before the strong ones in the reduplicative syllable only.

 [The](https://#%C2%A0 "लिट्यभ्यासस्योभयेषाम् । 6. 1. 17.") roots **व्रश्च्–प्रच्छ्** and **भ्रस्ज्** do not tako Samprasâraṇa in the Perfect.


[The](https://#%C2%A0 "व्यथोलिटि। 7. 4. 68. द्युतिस्वाप्योः सम्प्रसारणम्। 7. 4. 97.") roots **व्यथ** and **द्युत्** take Samprasâraṇa in the reduplicative syllable only before the strong as well as the weak terminations of the Perfect, **श्वि** takes Samprasâraṇa optionally in the Perfect and Frequentative.

 [The](https://# "वचिस्वपियजादीनां किति। 6.1.16.") roots **वच्–स्वप्–यज्–वप्–वह्–वस्–वे–व्ये–व्हे–वद्** and **श्वि** take Samprasâraṇa before the weak terminations of the Perfect, Benedictive, Passive forms, Participle and Gerund; while the roots [**ग्रह्–ज्या–वय्**](https://%C2%A0# "ग्रहिज्यावयिव्यधिवष्टिविचतिवृश्चतिपृच्छतिभृज्जतीनां ङिति च 6.1.16.") (substitute for **वे**)**–व्यध्–वश्–व्यच्** undergo the same change as above and also before the weak terminations of the conjugational tenses and Frequentative **व्रश्च्–प्रच्छ्** and **भ्रस्ज्** do the same except in the Perfect.

**वच्** (Anit) 1. P. (also Atm. in non-conj. tenses) to speak.

(Inclnding the substitute of **ब्रू**).

**वे** (Anit) 1. P. 4. 'to weare, to sew.'

**
[वे](https://# "वेओवयि॥ II. 4. 41. लिटिः वयोपः॥ VI 1.38. वश्चास्यान्यतरस्यां किति॥ VI. 1. 39.")** substitutes **वय्** optionally in tho Perfect. **य्** of **वय्** does not take Sâmprasarana in the Perfect. **य्** of **वय्** takes **व्** as its substitute optionally before the weak terminations of the Perfect **वय्** is Set and it admits **इ** necessarily before **थ**.

*Parasmaipada.*

|:------:|:------------:|:-------------:|:-------------:|

| 2\. | **ऊयिषे–ऊविषे** | **ऊयाथे–ऊवाथे** | **ऊयिध्वे–ढ्वे–ऊविध्वे–ढ्वे** |
| 3\. | **ऊये–ऊवे** | **ऊयाते–ऊवाते** | **ऊयिरे–ऊविरे** |

 According to 196 (*b*) **वे** has the following forms.

*Parasmaipada.*

| | | | |
|:---:|:-------------:|:--------:|:--------:|

| 3\. | **ववौ** | **ववतुः** | **ववुः** |

| | | | |
|:---:|:--------:|:---------:|:------------:|
| 1\. | **ववे** | **वविवहे** | **वविमहे** |
| 2\. | **वविषे** | **ववाथे** | **वविध्वे–ढ्वे** |
| 3\. | **ववे** | ** ववाते** | **वविरे** |

[व्ये](https://#%C2%A0 "न व्यो लिटि VI. 1. 46॥ इडत्यर्तिव्ययतीनाम् VII. 1. 66.") (Anit) 1. P. A. 'to cover, to sew.'

 The finaly **ए** of **व्ये** is not replaced by **आ** in the Perfect **व्ये **admits of **इ** necessarily before **थ**.

 The modified base of **व्ये** is **विव्यय्** before the strong, and **विवी** before the weak terminations, the **ई** of final **वी** in the latter case changing to **य्** by virtue of rule 123.

**द्युत्** (Set) 1. A. 'to shine.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:-----------:|:------------:|:------------:|
| 1 | **दिद्युते** | **दिद्युतिवहे** | **दिद्युतिमहे** |
| 2 | **दिद्युतिषे** | **दिद्युताथे** | **दिद्युतिध्वे** |
| 3 | **दिद्युते** | **दिद्युताते** | **दिद्युतिरे** |


[(201)](https://# "अतएकहल्मध्येऽनादेशादेर्लिटि॥ VI. 4. 121. थलि च सेटि॥ VI. 4. 120.") When a root having an **अ** between two simple consonants does not change its reduplicative syllable, the **अ** is changed to **ए** and the reduplicative syllable dropped when followed by the weak terminations of the Perfect. When the **थ** of the 2nd person singular Parasmaipada takes the augment **इ** optionally, the above change takes place only when it takes **इ** and not when it [does](https://# "अतएकहल्मध्येऽनादेशादेर्लिटि॥ VI. 4. 121. थलि च सेटि॥ VI. 4. 120.") not. The following Anit and Wet roots answer all the conditions in the rule.

*(a) Anit Roots*

**शक्** 5 P. 'to be able.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:-------------:|:--------:|:--------:|
| | S. | D. | P. |
| 1\. | **शशाक–शशक ** | **शेकिव** | **शेकिम** |
| 2 | **शेकिथ–शशक्थ** | **शेकथुः** | **शेक** |
| 3\. | **शशाक** | **शेकतुः** | **शेकुः** |

**पच्‌** 1. P A. ‘to cook’

*Parasmaipada.*

| | | | |
|:---:|:------------------------------------------:|:--------:|:--------:|
| 1\. | **पपाच–पपच** | **पेचिव** | **पेचिम** |
| 2\. | **पेचिथ–[पपक्थ](https://#%C2%A0 "by (84)")** | **पेचथुः** | **पेच** |
| 3\. | **पपाच** | **पेचतुः** | **पेचुः** |

*Atmanepada.* 

| | | | |
|:---:|:--------:|:---------:|:---------:|

*(b) Wet Roots.*

** रध्‌** 4 P. ‘to kill, to subdue, to cook’ inserts **न्** before a vowel. Hence there are only two forms by the above rule, viz, **रेध्व** and **रेध्म.**

| | | | |
|:---:|:---------------:|:--------------:|:--------------:|
| 1 | **ररन्ध** | **ररन्धिव–रेध्व** | **ररन्धिम-रेध्म** |
| 2\. | **ररन्धिथ–ररद्ध** | **ररन्धथुः** | **ररन्ध** |
| 3 | **ररन्ध** | **ररन्धतुः** | **ररन्धुः** |

**नश्** 4. P. ‘to vanish.’

| | | | |
|:---:|:-------------:|:------------:|:------------:|
| 1\. | **ननाश–ननश** | **नेशिव–नेश्व** | **नेशिम–नेश्म** |
| 2\. | **नेशिथ–ननंष्ट** | **नेशथुः** | **नेश** |
| 3\. | **ननाश ** | **नेशतुः** | **नेशुः** |

Exceptions to Rule (201).

 [(1)](https://#%C2%A0 "न शसददवादिगुणानाम्‌ VI. 4. 126.") The roots **दद्** and **शस्.**

**दद्** (Set) 1 A, ‘to give, to present.’

| | | | |
|:---:|:---------:|:----------:|:----------:|
| | S. | D. | P. |
| 1\. | **दददे** | **दददिवहे** | **दददिमहे** |
| 2\. | **दददिषे** | **दददाथे** | **दददिध्वे** |
| 3\. | **दददे** | **दददाते** | **दददिरे** |

**शस्** (Set) 1. P. 'to kill.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:------------:|:---------:|:---------:|
| 1\. | **शशास–शशस** | **शशसिव** | **शशसिम** |
| 2\. | **शशसिथ** | **शशसथु** | **शशस** |
| 3\. | **शशास** | **शशसतुः** | **शशसुः** |

 (2) The roots **जन्** and **दय्** for which see 199 and 211 respectively.

 (3) The roots of the 10th conjugation take the Periphrastie Perfect and therefore though some of the roots answer the conditions of this rule they do not follow it.

 (4) Roots beginning with **व** and the roots having an **अ** from a Guna change.

**वम्** (Set) 1. P 'to vomit, to, emit, to reject.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:------------:|:---------:|:---------:|
| | S. | D. | P. |
| 1 | **ववाम–ववम** | **ववमिव** | **ववमिम** |
| 2\. | **ववमिथ** | **ववमथुः** | **ववम** |
| 3\. | **ववाम** | **ववमतुः** | **ववमुः** |

 Counter-exception–The Anit roots **वच्–वप्–वस्–वह्** and the Set roots **वद्‌** and **वश्** for all of which see section 200.

 [(5)](https://# "तॄृृफलभजत्रपश्च ॥ VI. 4 122. राधोहिसायाम् VI. 4. 128.") The roots **तॄ–फल्–भज्–त्रप्** and **राध्‌** meaning 'to kill' or **अपराध्** 'to offend' though not fulfilling the conditions of the rule, drop their reduplicative syllable and change the **अ** or **आ** to **ए** necessarily.

**तॄ** (Set) 1 P 'to cross, to swim.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:------------:|:--------:|:--------:|
| 1 | **ततार–ततर** | **तेरिव** | **तेरिम** |
| 2\. | **तेरिथ** | **तेरथुः** | **तेर** |
| 3\. | **ततार** | **तेरतुः** | **तेरुः** |

| | | | |

| 1 | **पफाल–पफल** | **फेलिव** | **फेलिम** |
| 2\. | **फेलिथ** | **फेलथुः** | **फेल** |
| 3\. | **पफाल** | **फेलतुः** | **फेलुः** |

| 3\. | **अपरराध** | **अपरेधतुः** | **अपरेधुः** |

 **राध्‌** ‘to kill’ has these same forms dropping the preposition **अप** all through.

 But **राध्‌ **4. P 'to grow' & 5. P. 'to accomplish' has the following forms.

|:---:|:----------:|:----------:|:----------:|

| 3\. | **रराध** | **रराधतुः** | **रराधुः** |

 (6) [The](https://# "वा जृभ्रमुत्रसाम्‌ VI. 4 124 फणा च सप्तानाम्‌॥ VI. 4 125.") roots **जृ–भ्रम्–त्रस्–फण्–राज्–भाज्–भाश्–भ्राश्–म्लाश्–स्यम्** and **स्वन्** undergo the above changes optionally.

| 2 | **सस्यमिथ–स्येमिथ** | **सस्यमथु–स्येमथुः** | **सस्यम–स्येम** |
| 3\. | **सस्याम** | **सस्यमतुः –स्येमतुः** | **सस्यमुः–स्येमुः** |

**स्वन्** (Set) 1 P ‘to sound, to hum, to sing.'

| | | | |
|:---:|:----------------:|:----------------:|:----------------:|
| 1\. | **सस्वान–सस्वन** | **सस्वनिव–स्वेनिव** | **सस्वनिम–स्वेनिम** |
| 2\. | **सस्वनिथ–स्वेनिथ** | **सस्वनथुः–स्वेनथुः** | **सस्वन–स्वेन** |
| 3\. | **सस्वान** | **सस्वनतुः–स्वेनतुः** | **सस्वनुः–स्वेनुः** |

 (7) When **श्रन्थ्, ग्रन्थ्** and **दम्भ्** drop their nasal according to 195_(/8), they drop their reduplicative syllable and change the **अ** to **ए** before the strong as well as the weak terminations of the perfect.

| 2 | **शश्रन्थिथ–श्रेथिथ** | **शश्रन्थथुः– श्रेथथुः** | **शश्रन्थ–श्रेथ** |
| 3\. | **शश्रन्थ–श्रेथ** | **शश्रन्थतुः–श्रेथतुः** | **शश्रन्थुः–श्रेथुः** |

THE PERIPHRASTIC PERFECT.

 (209) The Periphrastic Perfect is formed by affixing **आम्** to the root and then appending the Reduplicate Perfect Parasmaipada forms of **भू** or **अस्** after both Parasmaipada as well as Atmanepada verbs, or by adding the Reduplicate Perfect Parasmaipada forms of **कृ** after Parasmaipada verbs and the Reduplicate Perfect Atmanepada forms of **कृ** after Atmanepada verbs.

 (210) The final vowel and the penultimate short of roots take their Guna substitute before the **आम्** of the Periphrastic Perfect except that of **विद्**, **दीधी** and **वेवी**.

**इन्ध्** (Set) 7. A. 'to kindle, to shine.'

[TABLE]

1st Person Singular.

**ईड्** Set 2. A. to praise.

 **ईढाञ्चक्रे** or **ईडामास** or **ईडाम्बभूव** &c.

**ईड्** Set. 10. U. to praise.

 **ईडयाञ्चकार–चकर–चक्रे ईडयामास ईडयाम्बभूव **&c.

**ऊह्** Set. 1. P. to sprinkle.

CHAPTER XII.  
The Aorist *i.e.*, **लुङ्** or **अद्यतनीवृत्तिः **

 215. The personal terminations in the Aorist underg certain peculiarities and it may, therefore, be classified into the Radical Aorist and the Sibilant Aorist. In the Radical Aorist the terminations are added immediately to the root or to a base prepared by the addition of **अ** to the root, while in the Sibilant Aorist **स्** or **सिष्** or **स्** is prefixed to the terminations before adding them to the root.

 There are thus seven varieties in the Aorist out of which the 1st and the 6th ones are Parasmaipadi only.

*Parasmaipada.*

 The Parasmaipada Terminations of II and III varieties are the same as those of the Imperfect Tense (**लङ्**). For the VII variety they are the same, but **स** is prefixed to them; for the terminations **साव–साम–सम्** and **सन्** see sections 10 (a) and 10 (b).

 The Parasmaipada Terminations of the remaining varieties viz. for I, IV, V, and VI ones are the same as those of the Imperfect Tense with **उस्** for **अन्** as the third person plural termination. But in IV variety **स्**, in V **इष्** (this **इ**, it will be remembered, is the same **इ** which Set roots take, see section 185) and in VI **सिष्** are prefixed to the terminations. The second and third person singular terminations for IV and VI varieties are **सी** and **सीत्** and for V variety **ई** and **ईत्. **

*Atmanepada. *

 The Atmanepada Terminations for II and III Varieties are he same as those applied to the roots of the first class of conjugations but the 4th, 5th and 7th varieties take those for he second class of conjugations with the exception of the third person plural termination for VII variety which has **न्** prefixed to the final **त. **

** स्–इष् **and **स** are to be prefixed to the terminations in IV, V, and VII varieties **सि** the first person singular termination for VII variety is irregular.

 There are thus three varieties of the Radical Aorist viz I, II and III, and four Varieties of the Sibilant Aorist, viz. IV, V, VI and VII.

 (216) The following are the Sets of terminations for the even varieties.

First variety (only Parasmaipadi)

| | | | |
|:---:|:------:|:-------:|:------:|
| | S. | D. | P. |
| 1 | **अम्** | **व** | **म** |
| 2 | **स्** | **तम्** | **त** |
| 3 | **त्** | **ताम्** | **उस्** |

Second and Third Varieties.  
*Parasmaipada. Atmanepada.*

| | | | | | | | |
|:---:|:------:|:-------:|:------:|:---:|:-------:|:--------:|:-------:|
| | S. | D. | P. | | S. | D. | P. |
| 1 | **अम्** | **व** | **म** | 1 | **इ** | **वहि** | **महि** |
| 2 | **स्** | **तम्** | **त** | 2 | **थास्** | **इथाम्** | **ध्वम्** |
| 3 | **त्** | **ताम्** | **अन्** | 3 | **त** | **इताम्** | **अन्त** |

*Parasmaipada. Atmanepada.*

| | S. | D. | P. | | S. | D. | P. |

| 2 | **सी** | **स्तम्** | **स्त** | 2 | **स्थाः** | **साथाम्** | **ध्वम्** |
| 3 | **सीत्** | **स्ताम्** | **सुः** | 3 | **स्त** | **साताम्** | **सत** |

| 3 | **ईत्** | **इष्टाम्** | **इषुः** | 3 | **इष्ट** | **इषाताम्** | **इषत** |

| | | | | | | | |
|:---:|:------:|:--------:|:-------:|:---:|:--------:|:---------:|:---------:|
| 1 | **सम्** | **साव** | **साम** | 1 | **सि** | **सावहि** | **सामहि** |
| 2 | **सः** | **सतम्** | **सत** | 2 | **सथाः** | **साथाम्** | **सध्वम्** |
| 3 | **सत्** | **सताम्** | **सन्** | 3 | **सत** | **साताम्** | **सन्त** |

 (217). Some of the Set, Wet, and Anit roots take either of I, II, III, VI, and VII varieties exclusively, some optionally, while, others take certain varieties in the Parasmaipada only. In the Atmanepada, they take the 4th or the 5th variety according as they are Anit or Set, or if they are Wet they take both varieties. These will be noted down further on. But as a general rule Anit roots take the fourth variety, Set roots the fifth, and Wet roots take both viz. 4th and 5th varieties.


[(218)](https://# "लुङ्–लङ्–लृङ्क्ष्वडुदात्तः VI. 4. 71. आडजादीनाम् VI. 4. 102.") The augment **अ** or **आ** is prefixed to the roots in this tense as in the Imperfect. See section 14 and 14 (a).

FIRST VARIETY.

 (219). The ending **आ** of a root is dropped before **उस्** and the root **भू** takes **अन्** instead of **उस्** in the third person plural as in the Imperfect.

 (220). The roots enumerated in the following Karikas belong to the First variety.

**[गाति](https://#%C2%A0 "च्लि लुङि III. 1. 43 च्ले सिच् III. 1. 44. गातिस्थाघुपाभूम्यः सिचः परस्मैपदेषु II. 4. 77. विभाषा घ्रावेट्शाच्छासः II. 4. 78.")रधीगिणादेशो तिष्ठतिर्द्यतियच्छती।  
ददाति पिबतिर्भूधौ लगुष्ठानां सिचः सदा॥१॥**

**जिघ्रतिर्धयतिश्चैव श्यतिच्छ्यती स्यतिस्तथा।  
सिचोलुग्वा तु पञ्चानां परस्मैपदिनां लुङि॥२॥ **

 The roots **इ** (2. P. to go), **स्था**, **दो** (4. P. to cut), **दा** (1 P to give ), **दा** (3. P. A. to give ), **पा** (1. P. to drink), **भू** (1. P. to be) and **धा** (3. P. A. to hold) take the First Variety necessarily, and the roots **घ्रा** (3. P. to smell), **धे** (1. P. to drink), **शो**, **छो**, and **सो** assuming the forms of **शा**, **छा**, and **सा** in virtue of rule 196 (b) belong to this variety optionally. The root **इ** substitutes [**गा**](https://#%C2%A0 "इणोगालुडि II. 4. 51.") in the Aorist. The root **दे** (1. A to protect) though belonging to the [**घु**](https://#%C2%A0) verbs is omitted since it is Atmanepadi, and the root **धे** (1 P. to drink) is excluded from the **घु** verbs which belong to this variety necessarily, only because it is included among those that belong optionally **भू** becomes **भूव्**, see section 195 (3).

**इ** (2.P. to go)

| | | | |
|:---:|:--------:|:----------:|:--------:|
| | S. | D. | P. |
| 1 | **अगाम्** | **अगाव** | **अगाम** |
| 2 | **अगाः** | **अगातम्** | **अगात** |
| 3 | **अगात्** | **अगाताम्** | **अगुः** |

 The forms of **इ** with **अधि** 'to remember' would be **अध्यगाम्–अध्यगाव–अध्यगाम**, &c.

** स्था, दा** (1st and 3rd conj.) **पा, धा, घ्रा,** and **दो, धे, शो, छो,** and **सो** assuming the forms of **दा–धा–शा–छा** and **सा** are to be similarly conjugated.

 The forms of **छो** would be **अच्छाम्–अच्छाव–अच्छाम**, &c. and not **अछाम्–अछाव–अछाम** See 202 (a).

**भू** (1. P. to be).

| | | | |
|:---:|:--------:|:---------:|:--------:|
| 1 | **अभूवम्** | **अभूव** | **अभूम** |
| 2 | **अभूः** | **अभूतम्** | **अभूत** |
| 3 | **अभूत्** | **अभूताम्** | **अभूवन्** |

 (221) The roots **घ्रा, छो, शो** and **सो** take VI variety also.

 (222) **धे** takes III and VI varieties.

 (223) **दा–धा–स्था** and **इ** with **अधि** take IV variety in the Atmanepada.

 (224) **भू** when Atmanepadi takes V variety.

SECOND VARIETY.

 (225) In the second variety **अ** is added on to the roots before the terminations are applied. It is dropped before **अम्–अन्** and **अन्त** and lengthened before **व–म–वहि** and **महि**, see section 19 (a and b).

 (226) This **अ** is weak and the radical vowels, as a general rule, do not take Guna or Vridhi substitute.

 [Exception](https://#%C2%A0 "ऋदृशोऽङि गुणः VII. 4. 16.")—Roots ending in **ऋ** short or long and the **ऋ** of **दृश्** take Guna before the affix **अ** of the Second Variety.

 (227) This Variety is Parasmaipadi but in the case of the roots **ऋ** with **सम्** 3 conj, **ख्या** (**ख्य्**) tho substitute of **चक्ष्, वच्** (**वोच्**) (substitute of **ब्रू**); **अस्** (**अस्थ्**) with **परि** 4 conj. and [**लिप्**](https://#%C2%A0 "आत्मनेपदेष्वन्यतरस्याम् III 1.54. (a) आतोलोपइटि च VI. 4. 64. (b) पतः पुम् VI. 4. 19. अस्यतेस्थुक् VII. 4. 17. (c) शास इदङ्हलोः VI. 4. 34. शासिवसिघसीना च VIII. 3. 60. (d) श्वयतेरः VII. 4. 18."), **सिच्** and **ह्वे** (**ह्व**), it is Atmanepadi also.

 (228) The following irregularities regarding certain substitutes are to be carefully remembered.

 (*a*) The roots **ख्या** and **ह्वे** \[which is to be considered as a root ending in **आ** by virtue of rule 196 (*b*)\] drop the final **आ** before the weak affix **अ** of the second variety.

 (*b*) The roots **वच्** admits the augment **उ **before the affix **अ**.1.e., becomes **वोच्.** In the same way **पत्** takes **प्** and **अस्** 'to throw' **थ्**, and become **पप्त्** and **अस्थ्** respectively.

 (*c*) In the case of the root **शास्, इ** is substituted for the penultimate **आ** before the affix **अ** i.e. it becomes **शिस्** the **स्** of which becomes **ष्** as it is preceded by **इ**. The substitute for **शास्** is therefore **शिष्**.

 (*d*) **अ** is substituted for the final **इ** of the root **श्वि** before the affix **अ**.

 [(229)](https://#%C2%A0 "अनिदिता हल उपधाया क्ङिति VI. 4. 24.") The penultimate nasal of a root is, as a general rule, dropped when the root is followed by a weak termination. Hence in the second Variety the roots **भ्रंश्–**4 P. **स्तम्भ्–ग्लुञ्च्–बुन्द्–स्कन्द्–स्यन्द्–भ्रंश्** 1. A. **–स्रंस्–ध्वंस्–भ्रंस्** and **स्रम्भ्** drop their nasal.

 (230) The roots which are conjugated in this Variety are here grouped into three karikas and they are easier to be remembered than long lists. The first karika comprises the roots which take the second Variety necessarily. The second gives the optional ones and the third is the list of roots which are all Atmanepadi but when they take the second Variety, they become Parasmaipadi.

\(a\) Necessary roots of the Second Variety.

**पततिः सर्पतिश्चैव गच्छतिर्घसतिस्तथा।  
ह्रयतिश्चोभयपदी धातवो भ्वादयः स्मृताः॥  
अदादौ वक्तिशास्ती च ख्यातिश्चाथ तृतीयके।  
इयर्तिश्च ससर्तिश्च तथोभयपदी विषि॥  
उच्लुट्स्विद्भिद्मदिक्लिदू क्ष्विद्सिध् क्षुध् शुध् क्रुधि गृधिः।  
ऋधी रधिडिपी चैव कुप्गुप्युप्रुप्लुपिस्तथा॥  
तुभ्लुभ्नभ्क्षुभ्शमितमी क्लंश्रम्दम्भ्रमक्षमिर्नशिः।  
भृशिर्भ्रशिवृशीकृश्तृष् तुष्दुष्पुष्हृष्रिषीरुषि॥  
प्लुष्व्युष्शुष्तस्दस्यतिश्चास्यतिर्यस्जस्मसिर्मुसिः।  
बिस्कुस्बुस्बस्द्रुह्यमुह्यौ स्निह्यतिस्नुह्यती तथा।  
चतुर्थकं शक्यतिश्च ह्येकोभयपदी स्मृतः॥  
स्वादौ शक्नोतिराप्नोतिस्तुदादौ मुञ्चतिः सिचिः।  
विन्दतिर्लिम्पतिश्चैव लुम्पति शद्सदी तथा॥  
पिनष्टिश्च शिनष्टिश्च रुधादावेव सम्मतौ।  
एते चतुरशीतिः स्युः लुङ्यङ्विकरणे सदा॥**

 [Of](https://#%C2%A0 "आत्मनेपदेष्वन्यतरस्याम्") these roots **लिप्–सिच्–**and **ह्वे** and the roots **मुच्** and **लुप्** take the fourth variety in the Atmanepada; the roots **शक्** and **विद्** which are said by some to be Set take both the fourth or fifth in the Atmanepada and **विष्** 3. P. A, 'to occupy' take the seventh variety in the Atmanepada.

| |
|:--:|
| **पत्** 1. P—1st Person. **अपप्तम् अपप्ताव अपप्ताम** |
| **[ह्वे](https://#%C2%A0 "ह्वे A 3rd per. sing. Fourth Variety अह्वास्त.") (ह्व)** 1. P— 1st Person. **अह्वम् अह्वाव अह्वाम** |

\(b\) Optional roots of the 2nd Variety.

**श्विर्म्रुच्म्लुच्ग्रुच्ग्लुचिर्ग्लुञ्चिर्दृशि स्फुट्श्च्युत्च्युतिः श्चुतिः।  
स्कन्दिर् घुषिर् बृहिश्चैव तुहिर् दुहिरुहिस्तथा।  
अथोभयपदीबुन्दिर् बुधिश्चभ्वादयः स्मृताः॥  
रौतिर्निजिर् विजिश्चैव जॄतृप्दृप् श्लिष् शुचिस्तथा।  
स्तम्भुश्र्चविच् रिच्युज्भिद्छिद्छृद्क्षुद्रुध्तृद्रुधादयः॥  
सप्तत्रिंशत्स्वेषु ये वै परस्मैपदिनो यदा।  
तदा लुङ्यङ् विकरणा विकल्पेन भवन्ति हि॥**

 Of these 37 roots, 23 are Set, 2 Wet, and 12 Anit roots. Their other forms made up in the fourth, fifth, or both varieties are given under each root.

Set Roots.

 These roots take the second and fifth varieties, **श्वि** takes the third also.

[TABLE]



[TABLE]

Anit Root.

 These roots take the second and fourth varieties **श्लिष्** in the sense of 'to stick' takes the second, and when it means 'to embrace', it takes the seventh variety.

[TABLE]

 (c) Roots Parasmaipadi only in the Second Variety.

**रुच् घुट्रुट्लुट्लुठ्द्युत्श्वित्वृत् मिद्क्ष्विद्स्यन्द् स्विद् वृधिः शृधिः।  
क्लृपशुभ्क्षुभ्तुभ् भ्रंशिनभी स्रंसुध्वंसू भ्रशिस्तथा॥  
भ्रंसुस्रम्भू प्रथमके रुचादेः पञ्चविंशतिः।  
आत्मनेपदिनी नित्यं लुङीयन्तु विभाषया।  
यदा परस्मैपदिनी तदाङ्गिकरणा स्मृताः॥ **

 These roots though Atmanepadi are conjugated in the Parasmaipada in the II Variety. In the Atmanepada all of these

roots except **स्यन्द्** and **क्लृप्‌** take the fifth variety as they are Set.

 The roots **स्यन्द्** and **क्लृप्** are Wet and they therefore take both the fourth and fifth varieties.

Set Roots. 

[TABLE]

THIRD VARIETY.

 (231) The Aorist forms of roots of the tenth conjugation, causals, and certain denominatives are made up in the Third Variety.

 Exception: (a) [**श्रि**](https://#%C2%A0 "णिश्रिद्र्स्रुभ्य कर्तरि चङ् III. 1. 48.") 1. P. A., **द्रु** 1 P., **स्रु** 1. P. (if expressing the agent) and the root [**कम्**](https://# "कमे श्च्लेश्चङ् वक्तव्यः ॥") 1. A. when it does not take **अय्,** take this variety in the primitive form necessarily. The ending **इ** and **उ** of these roots is changed to **इय्** and **उव्** before the augment **अ** or of the third variety, and the root **कम्**, though Set, does not take V variety.

 (b) [The](https://#%C2%A0 "विभाषा धेट्श्वोः III. 1. 49.") roots **धे** and **श्वि** 1. P. take this variety optionally. The root **धे** assuming the form of **धा** by virtue of 196 (b) drops its **आ **after reduplication, and the root **श्वि **takes Samprasârana optionally in the Aorist of the causal, viz. it is to be taken as **शु.** For the other forms of **धे** see I and VI varieties and for those of **श्वि** II and V varieties.

 (232) This variety is both Parasmaipadi and Atmanepadi, the terminations are the same as those of II variety, before which **अ** is added on to the roots as in the second variety.

 (233) The root is reduplicated in the Third variety.

 (234) **श्रि **1. P. A. 'to depend upon', ' to serve'.

 (235) To form the Aorist of roots of the tenth conjugation and causals, the following rules are to be attended to–

 (*a*) The Vikarana **अय **of the tenth conjugation and causals to be added to the primitive root is dropped but the vowel changes are to be retained.

 (*b*)[^72] Roots with a penultimate short **ऋ **retain it optionally and with a long **ॠ **optionally shorten it See (237)

[^72]: # "उर्ऋत् VII 4. 7. उपधायाश्च VII 1 108"

 Exception–The roots **कृ–स्पृह्–गृह्–and मृग्** These are roots and not roots ending in consonants. See section (238)

 (c)[^73] The penultimate long vowel is shortened (**ए, ऐ** and **ओ, औ** are shortened to **इ** and **उ** respectively).

[^73]: # "णौ चड्युपधाया हस्व VII. 4.1."

 Exception,[^74] (1) Roots called (a) **अदन्त **viz. those written in the Dhātupātha as ending in **अ**, the root (b) **शास्**, the roots (c) marked with **ऋ**, and the roots (d) from which a vowel has been dropped, do not shorten their penultimate vowel in this varirty. See sections 238, 239, 240 and 241

[^74]: # "नाग्लोपिशास्वृदिताम् VII 4 2."





# Exception (2)[^75]–The roots **भ्राजू–भ्रास्–भाष्–दीप्–जीव्–मील्** and **पीड्** shorten their penultimate vowel optionally in this variety. See section 242.

[^75]: # "भ्राज भास भाष दीप जीव मील पीडामन्यतरस्याम् VII. 4. 3."

# Exception (3)[^76]–The roots **कण्–रण्–भण्–श्रण्–लुप्–हेद्–ह्वे–वण्–लुट्–लुप्–चण्** and **लुट्** do the same in the Aorist of the causal. See section 243

[^76]: # "काण्यादीना वेति वक्तव्यम्."

# (d)[^77] Then the root is reduplicated

[^77]: # "चडि VI. 1. 11."

# (e)[^78] If the reduplicative syllable be followed by a short or a prosodially short syllable, **इ** is substituted for **अ** in the reduplicative syllable.

[^78]: # "सन्वल्लघुनि चड् परेऽनग्लोपे VII 4. 93. सन्यत. VII. 479."

# Exception (1)[^79]–In the case of the roots **स्मृ–दृ–त्वर्–प्रथ्–म्रद्–स्तृृ** and **स्पश्,** the अ in the Reduplicative syllable is retained. See section 244.

[^79]: # "अत्स्मृदृत्वरप्रथम्रदस्तॄस्पशाम् VII. 4 95"

# Exception (2)[^80]–The **अ** in the reduplicative syllable of **वेष्ट्** and **चेष्ट्** is changed to **इ** optionally See section 245.

[^80]: # "विभाषा वेष्टिचेष्टयो. VII. 4. 96"

# Exception (3)[^81]–Roots ending in **उ** short or long substitute **उ** for **इ** in the reduplicative syllable if it be not followed by a letter of the labial class or a semi–vowel or **ज्** followed by **अ** or **आ** See section 246

[^81]: # "ओ पुयञ्ज्यपरे VII. 4. 80."

# Exception (4)[^82]–The roots **स्रु श्रु द्रु प्रु प्लु** and **च्यु** do it optionally. See section 247

[^82]: # "स्रवति शृणोति द्रवति प्रवति ग्लवति च्यवतीना वा VII 4 81"

#  (ƒ)[^83] The vowel of the Reduplicative syllable is lengthened, if it is short snd not prosodially long.

[^83]: # "दीर्घोलघौः VII. 4. 94."

# (238) The Illustration of Exception ¹/_((a)) to 235 (c)

# The following roots of the tenth conjugation are called **अदन्त** since they are written as ending in **अ** in the Dhātupātha They are therefore such roots as have a consonant for their penultimate. They are not roots ending in a consonant as they appear to be and the penultimate long vowel which appears after **अय्** dropped, is not shortened. Also they do not undergo the vowel changes noted in (235 e and f ) viz. no **इ** is substituted for **अ** in the Reduplicative syllable and its vowel is not lengthened. **धेक्–वल्क्–अङ्क्–विष्क्** have their forms as **अदिधेकत्–अववल्कत्–आञ्चकत्–अविविष्कत्. सुख्–दुख्** have **असुसुखत्,** &c. **मृग्–अङ्ग्** have **अममृगत्–आञ्जगत्. रच्–सूच्** have **अररचत्–असुसूचत् लज्** has **अललजत्. पट्–वट्–पुट्–कूट्–खेट्–खोट्–क्षोट्–**have **अपुपुटत्–अचुकूटत्,** –&c. **शठ्–श्वट्–**have **अशशठत्,** &c. **खेड्–दण्ड्–**have **आ–खेडत्–अददण्डत्. गण्–गुण्–कुण्–व्रण्–कर्ण्–वर्ण्–पर्ण्–** have **अजुगुणत्–अवव्रणत्–अपपर्णत्,** for **गण्–**see (250 b), **पत्–वात्–कर्त्–केत्**

**सङ्केत्** have **अववातत्‌–अचिकेतव्‌–अससङ्केतत्‌ पत्‌** has **अपीपत्–त** or **अपपतत्‌–त कथ्‌–श्रथ्‌–अथ्‌–तुत्थ्‌** have **अचकथत्‌–अशश्रथत् आर्तथत–अतुतुत्थत. गद्‌–पद्‌–छद्‌–छेद्‌** have **अपपदत्‌–अचच्छदत्‌–अचिच्छेदत्‌ अन्ध्–**has **आन्दधत्‌ ऊन्‌–ध्वन्–स्तन्‌–स्तेन्–**have **औननत्–अतिस्तेनत्** &c **क्षप्–कृप्–रूप्** have **अचकृपत,** &c. **भाम्–साम्–ग्राम्–सङ्ग्राम्‌–गोम्–स्तोम्–**have **अबभामत्‌–अससामत्‌–अजग्रामत्‌–अससङ्ग्रामत्–अनुगोमत्‌–अतुस्तोमत्‌. लाभ्‌–**has **अललाभत्‌, व्यय्–**has **अवव्ययत्‌; वर्–स्वर्–सार्–कुमार्–पार्–शूर्–वीर्–तीर्–कत्र्–सत्र्–चित्र्–सूत्र्–मूत्र्–छिद्र–मिश्र्** have **अचुकुमारत्–अससत्रत्–अपपारत्–अतितीरत्–अशु–शूरत्–अविवीरत्** &c. **कल्–काल्–आन्दोल्–शील्–वेल्–पल्यूल्–स्थूल्‌–प्रेङ्खोल्‌–**have **अचकालत्–अविवेलत्‌–आन्दुदोलत्–अपिप्रेङ्खोलत्–अतुस्थूलत्‌,** &c. **गर्व **has **अजगर्वत्, पष्‌–गवेष्‌–रूक्ष्** have **अरुरूक्षत्‌** &c. **अंस्–रस्–वस्–भाज्–सभाज्–वास्–निवास्‌** have **आंससत्‌–अबभाजत् **&c. **चह्–मह्–रह्–कुह्–स्पृह्–**and **गृह् **have **अचुकुहत्‌–अपस्पृहत्‌–अजगृहत्** &c.  


[TABLE]

 The following roots are marked with **ऋ** in the Dhātupātha. These do not shorten their penultimate vowel in the Aorist of the casual, viz. in the Third variety.

 **चकास्** 2. P, **वाश्** 4. A, **तुड्** 8. P, **लोक्–लोच्** 10.U, Parasmaipada roots of the 1st conjugation, viz **कब्; क्रीड्‌; निद्‌; पिस्‌; हुड्; हूड्‌; खाद्, द्राख्–ध्राग्व्–राग्व्–लाख्–शाग्व्–श्लाख्‌; केल्‌–खेल्‌–चेल्‌–पेल्‌–फेल्–वेल्‌–शेल्‌–क्ष्वेल्, मेथ्, ग्रेट्, ग्रेड्, रेव्, पेस्‌; ओख्; ओण्–शोण्–श्रोण्–श्लोण्‌; तोड्–रोड्–लोड्‌, धोर्‌; यौट्–रौट्; रौड् **and **शौद्.**

 Atmanepadi roots of the 1st conjugation.

 **जुत्–युत्–ढौक्, ट्क्–तिक्, विथ्;तिप्–स्तिप्, लोक्–श्लोक्, लोच् द्राघ्–ध्राघ्–राघ्–लाघ्–श्लाघ्, भाज्, द्राड्–ध्राड्–बाड्, गाध्‌–नाध्–बाध्; ताय्, शाल्; काश्– भ्राश्–भ्लाश्; कास्–तास्–भ्रास्** (242) **रास्; द्राह्–वाह्; टीक्–तीक्‌–शीक्–सीक्, क्लीब्–क्षीब्, चीभ्–शीभ्, द्रेक्–ध्रेक्–रेक्‌–स्रेक्, भ्रेज्‌–रेज्, हेड्; वेथ्, केप्–गेप्–ग्लेप्–तेप्‌–मेप्‌–रेप्–लेप्–वेप्‌–स्तेप्‌; रेब्; रेम्; खेव्–गेव्–ग्लेव्–तेव्–देव्–मेव्‌–सेव्, गेष्–ग्लेष्–जेष्–नेष्–पेष्‌–प्रेष्–येष्–रेष्–हेष्–ह्वेष्, जेह्–बेह्‌** and **वेह्**

 The following are the roots of the 1st conjugation, both the padas, **मिथ्, मिद्‌; चीव्‌, प्रोथ्; होड्, याच्‌, राज्‌, नाथ्, चाय्, दाश्; दास्‌, माह्; सेक्, एज्, रेट्‌; ग्लेट्‌, ग्लेड्; वेण्, नेद्‌, मेध्‌, वेन्, एष–भेष्‌–भ्रेष्** and **भ्लेष्**

**चेष्ट्** 1 A **(चेष्टयति–ते)** to act, to be busy. 3 **अचचेष्टत्** or **अचिचेष्टत्**

 (246) Exception 3 to 235 (e)

 The roots **हु–ह्नु–स्तु–नु–धू–दू–तु–द्यु–क्षु–क्ष्णु–कु–सु–**and **स्नु** substitute **उ** for **इ** in the Reduplicative syllable.

 The forms therefore are.–**अजूहवत्–त, अजुह्नवत्–त, अतुष्टवत्–त, अनूनवत्–त, अदूधुवत्–त** or **अदूधवत्–त, अदूदवत्–त्, अतूतवत्–त, अदुद्यवत्–त, अचुक्षवत्–त, अचुक्ष्णवत्–त, अचूकवत्–त, असूसवत्–त** & **असुष्णवत्–त.**

 The Reduplicative syllable of **रु–यु–लू–पू–भू** and **ज्यु** 1. A 'to go' does not change its **इ** to **उ**, as it is here followed by a letter of a labial class or a semi–vowel or **ज्** followed by **अ** or **आ.**

 The forms therefore are:– **अरीरवत्–अयीयवत्–अलीलवत्–अपीपवत्–अबीभवत्–**and **अजिज्यवत्–त.**

\(247\) Illustration of Exception 4 to 235 (e)

**स्रु** 1. P. **(स्रावयति–ते)** to go 3 **असिस्रवत्** or **असुस्रवत्**

**श्रु** 1. P **(श्रावयति–ते)** to hear 3 **अशिश्रवत्** or **अशुश्रवत्**

**द्रु** 1. P. **(द्रावयति–ते)** to go 3 **अदिद्रवत्** or **अदुद्रवत्**

**प्रु **1. A **(प्रावयति–ते)** to go 3 **अपिप्रवत्** or **अपुप्रवत्**

**प्लु** 1. A **(प्लावयति–ते)** to go 3 **अपिप्लवत्** or **अपुप्लवत्**

**च्यु** 1. A. **(च्यावयति–ते)** to go 3 **अचिच्यवत्** or **अचुच्यवत्**

 (248) Roots with initial vowels reduplicate the following consonant and add **इ** to it in the reduplicative syllable **आदयति–ते** (causal of **अद्** to eat), **आद्–अद्–अदिद्** and then **आदिदत्–त;**

 According to article 110 (a) **उन्द्, अर्ह्** and others form **औन्दिदत्** and **आर्जिहत्.**

 (249) The roots **अङ्क्, अङ्ग्, अन्ध् अंस्, ऊन्** and **अर्थ** have for the Aorist of their causal the forms **आञ्चकत्–त, आञ्जगत्–त, आन्दधत्–त, आंससत्–त, औननत्–त** and **आर्तथत.** See article 238

 (250) The root स्था[^85] substitutes **इ** necessarily for the penultimate vowel, and **घ्रा**[^86] does it optionally. **स्था** (causal **स्थापयति–ते**) by 235 (a) **स्थाप्,** by this rule **स्थिप्,** by 235 (d) **तिष्ठिप्–अतिष्ठिपत्. घ्रा** (causal **घ्रापयति–ते**), by 235 (a) **घ्राप्,** by this rule as well as by 235 (e) **घ्रिप्** or **घ्रप्;** by 235 (d) **जिघ्रप्** or **जघ्रप्,** by 235 (e) **जिघ्रप्**, and so there are two bases **जिघ्रिप्** and **जिघ्रप्–अजिघ्रिपत्** or **अजिघ्रपत् **

[^85]: # "तिष्ठतेरित् VII 4 5."

[^86]: # "जिघ्रतेर्वा VII. 4. 6"

(*a*[^87]) In the case of **पा** 'to drink' the penultimate vowel is dropped, and **ई** is added to the reduplicative syllable **पा** (causal **पाययति–ते**), by 235 (a) **पाय्;** by 235 (c) **पय्,** by 235 (d) **पपय्,** by this rule **पप्य्** and **पीप्य्–अपीप्यत् पा** 'to protect' is regular in its causal Aorist form as **अपीपलत्. **

[^87]: # "लोप पिबतेरीञ्चाभ्यासस्य VII. 4. 4."

(*b*)[^88] The root **गण्** or takes **इ** or **अ** in the reduplicative syllable **गण्** (causal **गणयति–ते**), by 235 (a) **गण्**, by 235 (d) **जगण्**, by this rule **जीगण्** or **जगण्**, **अजीगणत्** or **अजगणत्.**

[^88]: # "ई चगण. VII. 4. 97."

(*c*)[^89] The **ह्** of the Reduplicative syllable of **हि** 5 P 'to go' is not changed to **घ्** in this variety. The form therefore is–**हि** (causal **हाययति–ते**)**–हाय्–हय्–जहय्–जिहय्–जीहय्–अजीहयत्**

[^89]: # "हे रचडि VII. 3. 56."

(*d*)[^90] **स्वप्** takes Samprasarana in this form necessarily, and **श्वि** takes it optionally in this variety and the causal Desiderative.

[^90]: # "श्वापेश्चडि VI. 1. 18. णौ च सश्चङ्गो VI 1. 31."

**स्वप्–सुप्–सुषुप्–सूषूप्–असूषुपत्**

**श्वि–शु–शाव्–शशव्–शुशव्–शूशव्–अशूशवत्**

**श्वि** (causal **श्वाययति–ते); श्वाय्–श्वय्–शश्वय्–शिश्वय्–अशिश्वयत्.**

(*e*)[^91] The root **स्फुर्** substitutes **आ** optionally for the penultimate vowel. **स्फुर्** (causal **स्फोरयति–ते**) by 235 (a) **स्फोर्**; by 235 (b) **स्फुर्**, by this rule **स्फार्** optionally So there are two bases **पुस्फुर** and **पुस्फर्–अपुस्फुरत्** or **अपुस्फरत्**.

[^91]: # "चिस्फरोर्णौ VI. 1 54."

# (*f*)[^92] The causal Aorist of **इ** with **अधि** 'to study' is **अध्यापिपत्** or **अध्यजीगपत्**, of **इ** with **अधि** 'to remember' is **अध्यजीगमत्,** of **द्युत्** is **अदिद्युतत्,** of **ऊर्णु** is **और्णुनवत्,** and of **ईर्ष्य् **is** ऐर्षिष्यत्** or **ऐर्ष्यियत्**

[^92]: # "णौ च सश्चडो II. 4 51 द्युतिस्वाप्यो. सप्रसारणम् VII 4. 47. 1.3 91. द्युद्भ्योलुडि 1.3 91."

# **SIXTH VARIETY (only Parasmaipadi)**

# The 6th and 7th varieties are treated here before the 4th and 5th ones, it being more advantageous to do so

# (251) In this Variety terminations are directly applied to the roots.

# (252) Necessary and Optional roots of VI variety–

# **+[^93]यमादेशोयच्छतिश्व रमिःपर्याङ्व्युपादिक। नम्मीनातिमिनोतिश्चऽऽदन्तैजन्ताश्च धातवः॥ नित्यं सक्सिचिटश्चैषां लुडिज्ञेया मनीषिभिः॥१॥ लिनातिजिङ्घ्रतिधेट्शो छ्यतिस्यतीच धातव षट्वैसग्वेट्सिचौचात्न परस्मैपदिन स्मृताः॥२॥**

[^93]: # "यमरमनमाता सक् च VII 2. 78. विभाषा घ्राधेट्शाच्छास. II 4 78."

# The roots **यम्, रम्** with **परि–आ–वि** and **उप** and the roots **नम्, मी** 9 P 'to kill,' **मि** 5 P to throw, and the roots ending in **आ, ए, ऐ,** and **ओ** take the sixth variety necessarily in the Parasmaipada. The root **ली** 9 P. 'to adhere,' and the roots **घ्रा, धे, शो, छो** and **सो** take this variety optionally.

# (253) The roots **रम्, मि** 5 A, **मी** 9 A, take the fourth variety in the Atmanepada, and **ली** 9 P takes it in the Parasmaipada

# (*a*) For **घ्रा, शो, छो,** and **सो** see section 221 (page 234.)

# (*b*) For **धे** see section 222 and third variety.

 (*c*) For the roots **दो** 4 P to cut, **दा** 1 P. **दा** 3 P. **पा** 1 P. 'to drink' **स्था** and **धा** 3 P See section 220. 

 (*d*) The roots **दा **3. A **स्था** 1. A. and **धा** 3. A take the fourth variety in the Atmanepada.

 (254) The root **वे** 1.U. 'to weave' **ध्ये** 1 U. 'to cover, **हा** 3 P. to go, **हा** 3. A to abandon, and **ज्ञा** 9 U 'to know' take the sixth variety according to section (252) in the Parasmaipada, but in the Atmanepada they take the fourth variety.

 (255) The roots **गा** and **श्यै** 'to go,' **त्रै** and **दे** to protect, **मे** to return or exchange, **प्यै** to grow, all of the 1st conjugation, and the roots **मा** 3 4 to measure, though ending in **आ, ए** and **ऐ**, do not belong to this variety as all of these are Atmanepadi roots. They take the fourth variety being Anit.

 (256) The root **ह्वे** takes the second variety in both the Padas (see page 235) Besides it takes the fourth variety in the Atmanepada.

 (257) For **ख्या** see exception to section 196. It takes the second variety necessarily See section 228 (a)

 (258) The root **दरिद्रा** drops its **आ** optionally in the Aorist taking the sixth variety when it retains this **आ**, and the fifth one when it is dropped

 (259) Most of the Parasmaipadi roots ending in vowels that take this variety are given here.

 The roots **ज्या** 9 P, **द्रा**, **पा** to protect, **प्रा, प्सा, भा, मा, या, रा, ला, वा, श्रा, स्रा,** all of the 2nd conj and the roots **ध्मा, म्ना, कै, क्षै, गै, ग्लै, दै ध्यै, म्लै, श्रै,** and **स्त्यै,** all of the 1st conjugation take the sixth variety.

**SEVENTH VARIETY.**

 (260) The radical vowels do not undergo Guna or Vriddhi substitute in this variety

 (261) Necessary and Optional roots of VII variety

**\*[^94] कुशिस्त्विषिर्दिशिदिही दुहोद्विष्मेहती रिशिः।  
रुशोरुहिर्लिश्यतिश्च लिशतिर्विशतिर्लिहि॥  
एतेवेदाधिकदश लुङिनित्यक्सयोगिनः॥१॥  
निष्कुषि कर्षतिकृषी क्लिश्नातिर्विष्गुहिर्गृहि।  
तृहिबृही मृशिवृही श्लिष्यतिश्च स्तृहिस्पृशि॥  
लुडिक्सयोगिनो वैते धातवस्तु चतुर्दश॥२॥**

[^94]: # "शल इगुपधादनिट· क्स III. 1. 45. न दृश III 1. 48 स्पृशमृशकृषतृपदृपाच्ले सिज्वावाच्य।"



 Anit roots ending in **श्–ष्–स्** or **ह्** with a penultimate **इ–उ–ऋ** or **लृ**, take the seventh variety. **दृश्** is an exception, it takes II and IV varieties. Such of the Wet roots as answer the above rule take this variety optionally Fourteen of the Anit roots take this variety necessarily, and fourteen others including also some of the Wet roots take it optionally.

 (262) Of the optional roots **विष्** takes II variety in the Parasmaipada, and VII in the Atmanepada, **श्लिष्** when it means 'to embrace' takes VII variety, but when meaning 'to cling' it takes II one, the roots **कृष्, मृश्** and **स्पृश्** being Anit take IV, variety also, and the remaining roots viz **निष्कुष्–क्लिश्–गुह्–गृह्–तृह्–बृह्–वह्** and **स्तृह्** when they are Set take V variety, and when Anit they take VII variety instead of IV one, as they end in **श्–ष्–स्** or **ह्**

 (263) The root[^95] **दुह्–दिह्–लिह्** and **गुह् **when followed by the Atmanepada terminations with an initial consonant of the dental class viz. by the terminations **सावहि–सथा–सध्वम्** and **सत** drop optionally the **स** or **सा** and take only **वहि–था–ध्वम्** and **त** as their terminations in this variety.

[^95]: # " लुग्वा दुहदिहलिहगुहामात्मनेपदे दन्त्ये VII 3 73."

[TABLE]

**FOURTH VARIETY.**

 (264) Anit roots take IV variety necessarily and Wet ones optionally The exceptional peculiarities are noted further on.

 (265) The radical vowel takes its Vridhi substitute in the Parasmaipada.

 (266)[^96] In the Atmanepada the penultimate **इ–उ–ऋ–लृ** short or long, and the final **ऋ** of a root remain the same, while the ending **इ** or **उ** short or long takes Guna.

[^96]: # "लिड्सिचावात्मनेपदेषु 1. 2 11. उच्च 1 2 12."

  (267)[^97] Anit roots change their penultimate **ऋ** to **र्** optionally.

[^97]: # "अनुदात्तस्य चर्दुपधस्यान्यतरस्याम् VI. 1. 59."

 (268)[^98] **स्** is dropped when it is preceded and followed by any consonant except a nasal or a semi–vowel. It is also dropped when preceded by a short vowel and followed by any consonant except a nasal or a semi–vowel.

[^98]: # "झलोझलि VIII. 2. 26. हस्वादङ्गात् VIII 2. 27. "

 (269)[^99] The ending **स्** of a root when followed by any termination, beginning with **स्** and belonging to the non–conjugational tenses and moods takes **त्** as its substitute.

[^99]: # "सः स्वार्धधातुके VII. 4. 49."

**Anit Roots.**

 (270) Anit roots with the exception of those belonging to I, II, III and VI varieties must take IV variety necessarily. Some of the Anit roots that take the other varieties optionally or in the Parasmaipada only have their other or Atmanepada forms made up in this variety.

 The following Karikas enumerate the necessary and optional roots of the fourth variety.

**पचिर्भजिभुजीभ्रास्जिर्यज्रञ्चि खिद्तुदिर्नुदि।  
क्षिप्तप्वप्शप् नहिवही ह्येते द्विपदिन स्मृताः॥१॥**

**पृच्छतिस्त्यजतिश्चैव भञ्ज्मस्ज्रुज् सञ्ज्सृजिस्तथा।  
बध्नाती राध्व्यधि साधिश्छुप्स्वप्यभ् दंश्वसिर्दहि॥  
एते सप्तदशैव स्यु परस्मैपदि धातव॥२॥**

**स्वञ्ज् हद्बुध्ययुधिमनी तेपते रभतेलभि।  
वद्यविद्यौविनञ्चैव ह्यात्मनेपदि धातव॥  
त्रयश्चत्वारिशदेते नित्यंसिचिभवन्ति हि॥३॥**

**रिच्विज्निजिर्युज्विजिर् क्षुद्छिद्भिरुध्स्कन्दिदृशि॥  
स्पृश्मृश्कृष्मुच्सिचिगमी लिपिर्लुपियमीरमि॥  
लुङि सिज् यागिनो वै ते एकविंशति धातवः॥४॥**

 Note–The roots **मन्** 4. A–**बुध्** 4 A–**विद्** 4. 7 A–and **वस्** 1 P are Anit and take IV variety, but **विद्** 2 P–**मन्** 8 A–and **वस्** 2 P. are Set and take V variety only **बुध्** 1. P and **वस्** 4 P though Set take II variety exclusively **बुध्** 1st conjugation takes V variety in both the padas, and **विद्** 6 U being considered by some as a Wet root ought to take IV and V varieties, but it takes II variety in the Parasmaipada and V in the Atmanepada.

 The root **गम्**[^100] takes II and IV varieties, and **यम्** VI and IV ones **यम्**[^101] meaning "to marry" and **गम्** drop their nasal optionally in the Atmanepada fourth variety. **यम**[^102] meaning "to make known the faults of others" and **हन्**[^103] do the same necessarily **वध्**[^104] is substituted for **हन्** in the Parasmaipada necessarily and optionally in the Atmanepada. The substitute **वध्**[^105] takes V variety, and its vowel does not take Vriddhi

[^100]: # "वा गमं 1 2 13."

[^101]: # "विभाषोपयमने 1 2 16"

[^102]: # "यमो गन्धने 1 2 15"

[^103]: # "हन सिच् 1 2 14"

[^104]: # "लुडि च II. 4. 43 आत्मनेपदेष्वन्यतरस्याम् II. 4. 44"

[^105]: # "जनिवध्योश्च्य VII. 3 35"

**The Optional Roots**

 **रिच्विच्निजिर्युज्विजिर् क्षुद् छिद् भिद् रुध् स्कन्दिर्दृशि** take II and IV varieties, **स्पृश्–मृश्** and **कृष्** IV and VII, and **रम्** IV and VI varieties. The roots **लुप्** and **मुच्** 6th conjugation take II variety in the Parasmaipada and IV one in the Atmanepada. The roots **सिच्** and **लिप्** 6th conjugation do the same in the Atmanepada but take II variety not only in the Parasmaipada but in the Atmanepada also.

 (271) The root **पद्**[^106] substitutes **इ** necessarily for the termination **स्त**, the third person singular of the Aorist. It is optionally so substituted in the case of the roots **दीप्–जन्–ध–पूर्–ताय्**[^107] and **प्याय्.**

[^106]: # "चिणते पद III 1. 60."

[^107]: # " दीपजनबुधपूरीतायिप्यायिभ्योन्यतरस्याम् III 1 61"

[TABLE]

[TABLE]



[TABLE]



[TABLE]



[TABLE]

 Most of the Anit roots ending in vowels have been given here with their noteworthy exceptions in each case.

 (272) Anit roots ending in **आ** and those in **ए–ऐ** and **ओ** according to 196 (b).

 For Parasmaipada roots of this description see VI variety.

 **ली** 9 P assuming the form of **ला** by virtue of 196 (a) takes IV and VI varieties.

 Atmanepadi Roots such as **प्यै–त्रै–श्यै–मे** (all 1st conj) and the root **मा** 3rd and 4th conj take IV variety only **मा** and Parasmaipada takes VI variety.

 Roots belonging to both the padas such as **वे–व्ये**–(1. U), **मि** 5. U **मी, ज्ञा** 9 U and **हा** 3. U. take VI variety in the Parasmaipada and IV in the Atmanepada.

 Exception (1)–The roots **दा** 1. U. **धा** and **स्था** take the first variety in the Parasmaipada, and 4th in the Atmanepada **दे** 1. A. takes IV variety.

 Exception (2)–The root **ह्वे** takes II in the Parasmaipada and IV in the Atmanepada.

 The root **ख्या** which is a substitute for **चक्ष्** takes II variety only.

 (273)[^108] The vowel of the roots **स्था** and **घु** verbs viz **दा³–धा–दा¹–दो–दे** and **धै** (See page 233) takes **इ** as its substitute, and as it is weak, it does not take Guna or Vriddhi.

[^108]: # "स्थाध्वोरिच्च 1. 2. 17"

[TABLE]

\(274\) Anit Roots ending in **इ.**

 The roots **इ**. 1. P. to go, **क्षि** 1. 5 P, **धि** 6. P to hold, and **हि** 5 P, the root **स्मि** 1 A and the roots **चि** 5, **जि** 1, and **सि** 5. 9. to lie, (all both the padas) take IV variety.

 Exception—The roots **श्रि** and **श्वि** are Set, but **श्रि** takes III variety exclusively, and **श्वि** takes II, III and V varieties The roots **इ** 2 P. and **इ** with **अधि** 'to remember' take II variety, but **इ** with **अधि** 2. A 'to study' takes IV variety. In the last case गा is optionally[^109] substituted in the Aorist and the Conditional. The terminations to be applied to this **गा**[^110] and to the verbs of the **कुटादि** class are weak with the exception of those of the Causal, the **अ** of the Perfect and the affix **ञित्**. Again the vowel of this **गा** takes **ई** as its substitute according to the following rule.

[^109]: # "विभाषा लुङ्लृडो II 4. 50."

[^110]: # "घुमास्थागापाजहातिसा हलि VI. 4. 66."

 (275)[^111] The vowel of the **घु** verbs, **मा, स्था–गा–पा–हा** and **सो** takes **ई** as its substitute when followed by the consonantal weak terminations.  


[^111]: # "गाङ्कुटादिभ्योऽञ्णण्डित् 1. 2. 1."

[TABLE]



[TABLE]

\(276\) Anit Roots ending in **ई**

 The roots **भी–ह्री** (3 conj.), **क्षी–री–व्ली** (9), **वी** 2, **ई** 1, 2 and **ली** 1 (all Parasmaipadi), the roots **मी–प्री–पी–धी–दी–री–ली** and **ई** all of the 4th conjugation Atmanepada, and the roots **श्री–प्री–क्री** (9), and **नी** 1, both the padas, take IV variety.

 Exception–**शी** 2 A and **डी** 1 4 A are Set and take V variety. For **मि–मी** and **ली** 9 P. see 196 (a) and page 255  


[TABLE]

\(277\) Anit Roots ending in **उ**

 The roots **कु–तु–द्यु** (2 conj.), **हु** **³** and **दु** **⁵** (all Parasmaipadi); **ह्नु²; प्लु–प्रु–ज्यु–गु—दु–च्यु** and **कु** all of 1st conj Atmanepadi, and **श्रु–धु** (5), **यु** and **स्कु** (9) of both the padas take IV variety.

 \*Exception[^112] (1) The Anit Roots **द्रु** and **स्रु** take III variety exclusively.

[^112]: # "णिश्रिस्रुद्रुभ्य कर्तरिचङ् III 1.48."

 Exception[^113] (2). The Anit Roots **स्तु** 2 and **सु** 5 U take IV variety in the Atmanepada and V variety in the Parasmaipada

[^113]: # "स्तुसुधूञ्भ्य परस्मैपदेषु VIII 2. 72."

 Exception[^114] (3). The Anit Root **सु** 1, 2 Parasmaipada takes IV and V varieties.

[^114]: # "See page 176."

 Exception (4). The roots **यु–रु–क्ष्णु–नु–क्षु** and **स्नु** are Set and therefore take V variety. The root **स्नु** and **क्रम्**[^115] take IV variety in the Atmanepada and V in the Parasmaipada.

[^115]: # "स्नुक्रमोरनात्मनेपदनिमित्ते VII. 2. 36."

 (277 a) **गु** 6 P. and **कु** 6. A. 'to sound' belong to **कुटादि** class and the vowel therefore does not take Guna See 274.  


[TABLE]

\(278\) Anit Roots ending in **ऋ**.

 The roots **पृ 3–सृ–स्मृ–ह्वृ** (all 1 P), the roots **मृ–धृ–दृ–पृ** (all 6. A ), and the roots **भृ** 1 3, **कृ** 5.8 **हृ–धु–ऋ** (all 1 U.) take IV variety.

 Exception (1) The root **ॠ** 3 P. takes II variety.

 Exception (2).  Roots[^116] with a final **ॠ** which is preceded by a conjunct consonant take IV or V variety in the Atmanepada. The root **स्तृ** 5 U. is a root of this kind.  


[^116]: # "ऋतश्चसंयोगादेः VII. 2. 43"

[TABLE]



[TABLE]



[TABLE]

 For the Atmanepadi forms of the 5th Variety See section 286.

**SET ROOTS.**

 (279) **वृ**[^117] 9. A, **वृ** 5 U, and roots ending in long **ॠ** take IV or V variety in the Atmanepada

[^117]: # "लिङ्सिचेारात्मनेपदेषु VII. 2. 42."

**WET ROOTS.**

 (280) Of Wet roots **तञ्च्–तञ्ज्–मृज्–व्रश्च्–त्रप्–गाह्–तृह्–अक्ष्–तक्ष्–त्वक्ष्–सिध्** 1. P and **अश्** 5 A–**गुप्** I. P. and **क्षम्** 1 A take IV or V variety. The roots **क्लिद्–रध्–नश्–द्रुह्–मुह्–स्निह्–स्नुह्** and **सिध्–गुप्–क्षम्** (when these three roots are of the 4th conjugation) take II variety necessarily. **अश्** 9 P and **गुप्** 1 A being Set take only V variety. The roots **तृप्–दृप्–स्यन्द्** and **क्लृप्** II, IV and V, and the roots **क्लिश्–गुह्–तृह्–स्तृह्–वृह्** and **बृह्** take VII and V varieties. The root अञ्ज्[^118] takes V variety only

[^118]: # "अञ्जेः सिचि VII. 2. 71."

[TABLE]



[TABLE]



[TABLE]

 (281) The roots **स्वृ** 1 U, **धू**[^119] 5 9. U, and **सू** 2 4. A are Wet They therefore take both IV and V varieties, with the exception of **धू** which does not take IV variety in the Parasmaipada.

[^119]: # "See section 186."

[TABLE]

**FIFTH VARIETY**

 (282) Set roots with the exception of those that are restricted to I, II III, IV, VI, and VII varieties take V variety necessarily. The optional roots or the roots taking other varieties in the Parasmaipada only, have their other or Atmanepada forms made up in this variety.

***Parasmaipada.***

 (283) [^120]The ending vowel short or long of a root, the penultimate **अ**[^121] of roots ending in **र्** or **ल्**, and the radical[^122] vowel of **वद्** and **व्रज्** take Vriddhi necessarily in the Parasmaipada.

[^120]: # "सिचि वृद्धि परस्मैपदेषु VII 2. 1."

[^121]: # "अतोल्राज्तस्य VII 2 2."

** **(285) \*[^123]The intermediate **इ** is optionally lengthened in the case of **वृ** and roots ending in long **ॠृ** before the terminations of the non–conjugational tenses and moods except those of the Perfect. It is necessarily lengthened in the case of the root ग्रह्[^124] under the same circumstances. But it is not at all lengthened before the Parasmaipada terminations of V variety. Hence Parasmaipada froms of **वृ** are only **अवारिषम्**, &c

[^123]: # "वृतोवा VII. 2. 38."

[^124]: # "ग्रहोऽलिटिदीर्घ VII. 5. 37. सिचि च परस्मैपदेषु VII. 2. 40."

 (286) The root **स्तु** 5th conjugation takes V variety optionally in the Atmanepada. See exception 2 to section 278.

 (287) Vriddhi is optionally substituted for the final of **ऊर्णु** in the Parasmaipada.

[TABLE]

 (288)[^125] The intermediate **इ** is optionally weak in the case of the root **ऊर्णु.** Hence one base is **और्णव्** when the final **उ** of **ऊर्णु** takes Guna and the other base is **और्णुव्** as **उ** is changed to **उव्** before the terminations of V variety in this case specially.

[^125]: # "ऊर्णोतोर्विभषा VII 3.90. विभाषोर्णो 1.2.3."

 Note–अ is not lengthened in the Atmanepada.

 *Atmanepada.*

 (292) The final vowel and the penultimate short of roots take their Guna substitute in V variety in the Atmanepada

 (292a) The root विज्‌ 3 U. is Anit and take II and IV varieties विज्‌ 6 A and 7 P. is Set and takes V variety only, but the intermediate इ is weak in this case and the penultimate इ of विज्‌ does not therefore take Guna.

| सन् 8 U — | असा-सनीत्‌; | असनिष्ट-असात, | असनिष्ठा-असाथा |

 (294) ऻThe vowel of सन्‌ is lengthened before त and था (the optional substitutes of इष्ट and इठाः according to 293) after dropping its न् The forms are therefore असाथा and असात instead of असथा and असत.

\(B\) THE BENEDICTIVE MOOD आशीर्लिङ्  
(318) Terminations.

[TABLE]

  The ध् of सीध्वम्‌ is to be changed to ढ् by 189 (b), page 180.

 (319) The Parasmaipada terminations are weak except in the case of roots ending in short ऋ which is preceded by a conjuct consonant and the roots जागृ and ऋ 1. 3. P.

 (320) The Atmanepada terminations are the strong except in the case of Anit roots and roots ending in ऋ short or long when the terminations do not take इ, viz, the ending ऋ short or long of roots whether Set, Wet or Anit when they admit इ and the final vowels and the penultimate short of roots of all Set roots except गुर् 4. A. the penultimate vowel of Wet roots क्लृप् and गृह्

when they take इ and the final of सू and धू with or without इ and the ending इ—ई and g of Amit roots take Gunain the Atmanepada Benedictive See sections 333 a, 384 and 335.

*Parasmatpada.*

 (321) The Parasmaipada terminations of the Benedictive begin with य् and Set roots do not, therefore, take the augment इ (see section 185). Hence all roots whether Set, Wet or Anit do not take the augment इ in the Benedictive Parasmaipada.

Roots ending in vowels.

 (322) Roots ending in अ—ए—ऐ and ओ \[see 196 (b)\] and not preceded by a conjunct consonant retain the final आ before the terminations.

 Exception (1)—Roots ending in आ—ए—ऐ and ओ and preceded by a conjunct consonant change the final आ to ए[^128] optionally. The root दरिद्रा drops its आ before the terminations. The forms are दरिद्र्यासम्—दरिद्र्यास्व, &c

[^128]: # "वान्यस्यसयोगदे VI. 4. 68."

 Exception (2)—the घु[^129] verbs दा—धा (3. U) दा 1. P—दो—दे—घे (see page 233) and the roots मा—स्था—गै—पा to drink—हा 3. P. to abandon and सो change the ending आ to ए necessarily.

[^129]: # " एर्लिङि VII 4. 67."

 Exception (3) —The roots वे—व्ये—ह्वे and ज्या take Samprasarana and lengthen the vowel in the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive, viz वे and ह्वे substitute ऊ for बे, while ज्ये and ज्या substitute ई for ये and या The base, therefore, in each case becomes ऊ-हू-वी and जी.

 (323) The[^130] ending इ and उ of roots are lengthened before the weak terminations of the Benedictive Parasmaipada, and the य of the Passive, as ची and धू from चि and धु

[^130]: # "अकृत्सार्वधातुकयोर्दीर्घ VII 4. 25. "

 Exception (1):—The root इ ‘2. P.’ is not lengthened when it takes a preposition.

 Exception (2):—The root श्वि takes Samprasârana and lengthens the vowel in the Benedictive, and before the व of the Passive, the base becomes शू.

 Exception (3):—For मि or मी 5.9. U. and दी and ली 4. A see 196 (a).

 (324) Roots ending in
ऋ[^131] change it to रि, but if the ऋ be preceded by a conjunct consonant, गt takes Guna before the weak terminations of the Benedictave Parasmaipada and the य of the Passive, as क्रि from कृ, and स्मर् from स्मृ. The roots जागृ and ऋ 1 3 P. take Guna.

[^131]: # " रिड्शयशग्लिङ्क्षु VII. 4. 28. गुणोतिसंयोगाद्यो. । VII. 4 29."

 (325) Roots ending in long ऋ change it to ईर्‌ but if the ऋ follows a labial or व् it is changed to ऊर् before the weak terminations of the Benedictive Parasmaipada, and the य of the Passive, as स्तीर्‌ and वूर् from स्तृृ and वृृ

Roots ending in Consonants.

 (326) The roots वच्-स्वप्--यज्--वप्--वह्--वस्--वद्‌ ग्रह्—व्यध् वश्-व्यच्‌-व्रश्च्‌-प्रच्छ्‌ and भ्रस्ज्‌ take Samprasárana in the Parasmaipada only and before the य of the Passive. 

 (327) The roots दिव्—सिव्—ष्ठिव् and स्रिव् lengthen their penultimate इ before the terminations of the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive. See (246).

 (328) +The[^132] roots जन्-सन्‌ and खन्‌ optionally substitute आ for the final न् and the root ऊह्[^133] when with a preposition shortens its penultimate before the Parasmaipada terminations of the Benedictive and the य of the Passive.

[^132]: # " ये विभाषा VI 4. 48."

[^133]: # " उपसर्गाद्ध्रस्व ऊहते VII. 4 23."

 (329) The अय् of the Tenth Conjugation and Causals and the Denominative य् are dropped in the Benedictive Parasmaipada and retained in the Atmanepada. But it is to be remembered that those roots of the tenth conjugation whose final vowels and the penultimate अ take Vridhi and the penultimate short takes Guna in the conjugational tenses and moods undergo the same change in the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive.

 (330) The roots ज्ञा—वा—प्री and धू (all 10 U) retain their substitutes ज्ञाप—बाप्—प्रीण and धून् in the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive.

 (331) The penultimate nasal of the following Parasmaipadi roots is dropped in the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive:—

 अञ्च्‌ meaning ‘to go'—बञ्च्—कुञ्च्—लुञ्च्—सञ्ज्—स्कन्द्—तुम्प्—दंश् and शंस् (all 1. P.) रञ्ज्‌ 1. 4. P. —मन्थ् 1 9 P.—भ्रंश् 4. P.—दम्भ् 5. P.—स्कम्भ् and स्तम्भ् 5. 9. P.—तृंह् 6. 7 P—अञ्ज्—भञ्ज्—उन्द्—तञ्ज्—-and तञ्ज् (all 7. P) and ग्रम्थ्—श्रन्थ्—बन्ध् (all 9 P)

 Exceptions—

 (*a*) The root अञ्च्‌ meaning ‘to worship’ does not drop its nasal.

 (*b*) The penultimate nasal of all Atmanepada roots and that of the following Parasmaipada ones is invariably retained in the Benedictive and before the य of the Passive.—

 तक् and काङ्क्ष् (1. P.)—लिङ्ग्—लङ्घ्‌ (1. P.)—उञ्छ् 6 P. and वाञ्छ् 1 P—खञ्ज् and गुञ्ज् (1 P.), लुण्ट्—कुण्ठ्—लुण्ठ्—मण्ड्—मुण्ड्—क्रन्द्—क्लन्द्—क्लिद्—निन्द्‌—नन्द्‌—मन्थ्—and चन्द्‌ (all 1 P) गुम्फ् 6 P— चुब्—धिन्द् (1 P) and हिंस् 7. P.

 (332) The root जभ् 1 A takes a nasal in the Benedictive and in the Passive, as जम्भिषीय—जम्भिषीवहि, जम्भ्यते, &c.

*Atmanepada.*

\(333\) Set Roots take इ necessarily

 Exception—Roots ending in long ऋ and the root वृ 9. A. 5. U. take इ optionally in the Atmanepada Benedictive This intermediate इ is not l[^134]engthened in the Benedictive as in the Perfect, see section 285.

[^134]: # " न लिडि VII. 2. 39."

 (*a*) In the case of Set roots, final vowels, penultimate short of roots and the ending long ऋ of roots, when they take इ, take their Guna substitute in the Atmanepada Benedictive except the root गुर् 4 A. गुर् lengthens its penultimate instead of taking Guna.

 When roots ending in long ऋ do not take इ; it is changed to ईर्, or to ऊर् if a labial or व् precedes.

 (334) Anit roots do not take इ.

 Exception —Roots ending in short ऋ preceded by a conjunct consonant admit इ optionally.

 (*a*) Final इ—ई—उ and final ऋ preceded by a conjunct consonant when it admits इ take their Guna substitute, while roots ending आ—ए—ऐ—ओ \[observe 196 (*b*)\], roots ending in ऋ not preceded by a conjunct consonant and also in ऋ preceded by a conjunct consonant but when it does not take इ remain unchanged कृ and स्तृ are the instances.

“(335) Wet roots take g optionally.”

“ (*a*) All Set roots ending in long ऋ and the root वृ 9. A. 5. U. all Anit roots ending in short ऋ preceded by a conjunct consonant and the Wet roots क्लृप्”—“गृह्”—गुह्—स्वृ“ (all 1 A), सू 2 4 A and धृ 5 9. U take इ optionally inthe Atmanepada Benedictive  

 The roots सू and धू take Guna with or without इ. The roots वृ—क्लृप्-गृह् and स्वृ take Guna when with इ and remain”

unchanged when without इ, while the root गुह् lengthens its vowel instead of taking Guna when it takes इ and remains unchanged when without इ.

 (336) Observe 195 (1—4—7), 11 (c and I), 98, 24 (a), 277 (a), 288 and exception 2 to 306, regarding the following गुप्—धूप्—विच्छ्—पण्—ऋत्—कम्—चक्ष्—अज्—गुह्—कित्—बध्—दान्—शान्—मान्—तिज्—गुप् (1 A.)—शास्—कृृत्— (कीर्त्) कु 6 A. ऊर्णु—छृद्—तृद्—कू (कुव्‌)-हन् (वध्)—हा 1. A and पा 2 P. to “protect"

| 3 | देयात्‌ | देयास्ताम्‌ | देयासु. |

CHAPTER XV

THE PASSIVE VOICE AND THE IMPERSONAL CONSTRUCTION.

 (338) The Passive and Impersonal forms are formed in one and the same manner from all roots of the ten classes without any conjugational distinction. They, however, differ in their formation in the conjugational and non-conjugational Tenses and Moods 'The roots also undergo certain peculiarities before they take the terminations.

 (a) CONJUGATIONAL TENSES AND MOODS.

 (339) The Passive and Impersonal forms in the Conjugational Tenses and Moods are made up by adding **य** to the original root and then applying the Atmanepada terminations, whether the root is Parasmaipadi or Atmanepadi in the Active.

 (340) This **य** is weak, viz, no Guna or Vriddhi substitute takes place before it.

 Exception,—Roots of the tenth conjugation capable of taking Guna or Vriddhi substitute in the Active Voice, do the same in the Passive Also the roots **ज्ञा—वा—धु** and **पी** (all 10th conjugation) retain their substitutes **ज्ञाप्**—**वाप्—धून्** and **प्रीण्** before the **य **of the Passive.

Note the following radical peeulzarities.

 (341) Of roots endingin **आ**, the घु verbs viz **दा—धा** (3.U) **दा** 1. P. **दो—दि**—(see page 233 and see 196 (b) and the roots मा—स्था—गै—पा to dnuk—**हा** to abandon and **सो** see page 264 and see 196 (b)? change the ending **आ** to **ई **before the **य** of the Passive The ending **आ** of other roots and the **आ** to be substituted in the case of roots ending in **ए—ओ **and ऐ \[196 (b)\] remain unchanged

 (342) Observe exception 3 to section 322 regarding **वेव्ये——द्वे **and **ज्या** in the Passive also दारिद्रा drops its **आ** before य.

 (343) Roots ending in short **इ** and **उ**,in **ऋ **preceded by a simple or conjunct consonant and roots ending in long **ऋ** take

the same changes which they undergo before the Parasmaipadsa terminations of the Benedictive See sections 323, 324 and 325

 The root **शी **substitutes **अय्‌** for its vowel before weak terminations beginning with **य** and the roots **ऋ** 1, 3 P. and **जागृ** take Guna.

 (344) Of roots ending in consonants, those mentioned in section 326 and 331 take Samprasrana and drop their nasal before the **य** of the Passive also. **तन्‌** optionally substitutes **आ** for its final.

 (345) Of Atmanepadi roots having a penultimate nasal only **इन्ध्** 7 conj—**स्यन्द्—स्रंस्—स्रम्भ्‌** and **खञ्ज्** all 1 Conj, drop their nasal before the **य** of the Passive

 (346) Observe Sections 98, 327, 328, 195 (1-4-7)and 11 (e) regarding **शास्—दिव्—सिव्—ष्टिव्—स्रिव्—जन्—सन्—खन्‌ and. ऊह् With सम्‌, गुप्—धूप्—विच्छ्—पण्—पन्‌—ऋत्—चक्ष्—अज्—कित्—वध्—दान्—शान्‌—मान—तिज्** and **शप्** (1 A)

[TABLE]

[TABLE]

[TABLE]

NON-CONJUGATIONAL TENSES AND MOODS.

\(1\) THE PERFEHOYD.

 (348) The Passive of the Reduplicated Perfect is formed. by affixing the Atmanepadia terminations to every root whether it is Parasmaipadi or Atmanepadi in the Active as **गम्— जग्मे. यज्‌— इजे, भिद्—बिभिदे, अज्ज्— आनजे.**

 (349) The Periphrastic Perfect of the Passive is formed by affixing **आम्** to the root, and then appending the Atmanepada forms of three auxiliary verbs **अस्—कृ** and **भू** whether the root is Parasmaipadi or Atmanepadi, as **कथ्— कथयाञ्चक्र— बभ्रवे— कथयामास.**

\(2\) THE AORIST

 (350) The first and sixth varieties are exclusively Parasmaipadi All the roots belonging to them are Anit except the roots **भू** which is Set, **भू ** therefore takes Atmanepadi forms of the fifth variety in the Passive and Impersonal of the Aorist, and all the rest take those of the fourth variety.

 (a) The Atmanepadi forms of the second and third varieties are not used in the Passive and Impersonal of the Aorist Consequently roots belonging to them take the Atmanepadi , forms of the fourth, fifth or seventh varieties in the Passive and Impersonal of the Aorist according as they are Anit or Set,

 (b) The Passive and Impersonal forms of the fourth, fifth and seventh varieties of the Aonst are simply formed by appending the Atmanepada terminations to the prepared base

The Third Person Singular,

 (351) The third person singular of the Aorist Passive and Impersonal of all roots except **तप् **1 P and 4. A.is made up by prefixing to the root the augment and adding to it the termination **इ** instead or **स्त** or **सत**. The root **तप्** in the sense of "to repent" and in the reciprocal Passive too does not take **इ**

 (352) Before the Passive **इ** of the third person singular of the Aorist, the root takes the following changes—

 (a) The penultamate short of roots takes its Guna before the Passive **इ.**

 (b) Set roots ending in **म्‌** and the roots **वध्** and **जन्** do not lengthen the penultimate vowel before the Passive **इ**

 (c) The final vowels and the penultimate **अ** of Anit roots ending in **म् **viz of **गम्‌—नम्‌—यम्‌** and **रम्**, final of root **जागृ** and the penultimate **अ** of **चम्‌** with **आ-कम्** and **वस्** though these roots are Set, take Vriddhi before the Passive **इ.**

 (d) Roots ending in **आ** and 1 **ए-ऐ** and **ओ** \[ see section , 196 (b)\] take a before the Passive **इ.**

 e) The roots **रभ्—रध्—जभ्** and the root **लभ्** when with a preposition insert a nasal necessarily before the Passive **इ.**

 f) The root **लभ् **when without a preposition and the root **भञ्ज्** insert a nasal optionally and lengthen their **अ** when no nasal is inserted before the Passive **इ.**

 (353 ) The Passive and Impersonal forms of the Aorist of roots ending in a vowel, of roots ending in **अय्** (roots of the tenth class, Denominative, &c) and of roots **हन्—ग्रह्** and **दृश्** are optionally formed by adding **इ** to the root even when itis Amit exceptin the third person singular, and then appending the Atmanepada terminations of the fifth Aorist, before which the root undergoes the same changes as before the **इ** of the third

person singular of the Passive and Impersonal Aorist **इ** 'to go' substitutes **गा.**

 (354) Roots of the tenth conjugation drop **अय्‌** optionally in the Non-conjugational Tenses and Moods except in the Perfect,

 When **अय्** is dropped, the penultimate **अ** of roots of the nature of **कथ्—गण्—रच्—प्रथ्,** &c is optionally lengthened in the Passive of the Non-Conjugational Tenses and Moods.

 (3) THE TWO FUTURES, THE CONDITIONAL, AND THE BENEDICTIVE

 (355) The Passive and the Impersonal forms of the two ‘Futures, the Conditional and the Benedictive are formed simply by appending the Atmanepada terminations to the prepared base, whether the root is Parasmaipadi or Atmanepadi in the Active.

 (356) The Passive and Impersonal forms of the two Futures, the Conditional, and the Benedictive of roots ending in vowels and of roots **ग्रह्—दृश्** and **हन् **may optionally be formed by adding **इ** to the root even when it is Anit and then appending the Atmanepada terminations of the corresponding tenses and moods before which the root undergoes the same changes as before the **इ** of the third person singular of the Passive and Impersonal Aorist

PART IV.

 This part treats of the Derivative verbs \[See section4 l and c\] and the Participles, Gerunds, and Infinitives

CHAPTER XVI

\(a\) Causals. **(णिजन्ता).**

** **(358) Any root belonging to the ten Conjugational classes may take a Causal form conjugated in all the tenses and moods of the three voices. This form conveys the sense that a person or thing causes another person or thing to perform the action or το undergo the state denoted by the root  
 (359) The Causal base is made up by apprending **अय** to the root before the terminations are applied and making the same vowel changes as before the **अय** of the tenth conjugation The Jausal of roots of the 10th class is the same as the primitive

 (360) Roots ending in **आ—ए—ऐ** and **ओ** \[ see 196 (b)\] and the root **ऋ** 1. 3. P.—**ह्री** 3. P —**प्ली**.— 9 P **री ** 4 A 9 P—**क्नूय्—**1.A —**क्ष्माय् ** 1.A —**क्री** 9 U—जि 1 P— **मि** 5 U. **—मी** 9 .U. " to destroy"—**दी** 4 A—**इ ** 2 A " to study, "**स्मि** in the sense of " to astonish" and **वी** 2. P . When meaning " to cause to conceive," add on the augment **प्** before **अय**

 (a) The **य्** of **क्नुय्** and **क्ष्माय्** is dropped by the rule. **‘व्** or **य्** is dropped before any comsonant except **य्**’. The rooe **दरिद्रा** drops its final and does not take the augment **प्.** The roots **क्षै श्रा ** or **ग्लै** ‘to cook’ and **ज्ञा ** shorten their **आ** necessarily before **प्** and **ग्लै** and** स्ना** do it oprionally when not preceded by a preposition . The vowel of ** चि ** 5 10 U is optionally changed to **आचि** 10 U is** मित्** viz, it requires the pecultimate vowel to be short , consequently the optional froms are **चापयति-ते चपयति-ते**, regular ones being **चापयति-ते** and **चपयति-ते ** The root **स्मि** 1 A and 2P in usual senses of “to smile” ans “to go, to pervade” , & c are regular , as **स्माययति** “he causes a smile by” **वाययति** "he causes to go." &c.

 (361) The roots **शो—छो—सो—ह्वे—व्ये—वे—सै** 1 P. "to waste away " and
**पा** 1 P, " to drink " take the augment **य्** instead of **प्** before **अय.**

 (362) the root **पा** 2 P. " to protect " and **ला** 2 P when meaning " to melt " add before **अय.**

 (363) The root **वा** 2 P and **वै** 1 P when meaning " to shake or tremble" take the augment before **अय.**

 The root ला 2. P — **वै** 1.P in the senses other than those noted above and **वा ** 2 P. also form their causal regulary.

 (365) The root **प्री** and **धू** add **न्** before

  The root **ली** 4 A 9 P. as used in different senses and the root **भी** 3 P. become **लाप्—लाय्—लाल्—लीन्** and **भाय्—भाप्** and **भीष्** before **अय.**

 (365) The final vowels take Vriddhı substitute before **अय**, as **क्षायय** from **क्षि** 1. 5 P. and **क्षी** 9 P., **धावय** from **धु** 5 U. and **धू** 6 P; and **कारय** from **कृ** 8 U. and **कॄ** 6 P.

 Exception (1)—The roots **जागृ** 2 P. **स्मृ** 1 P. in the sense of 'to cause to long for, to regret' **दृ **9 P when meaning 'to fear' **नृृ** 9 P. meaning 'to guide' and **जृ** 4 P., and the roots **ऋ**—**ही**—**बी**—**री** take Guna substitute instead of Vrıddhı.

 Exception (2)— The roots **दीधी** and **बेबी** drop their final before **अय**. The root **इ** 2. P. with **प्रति** "to understand" is regular, but **इ** 2 P "to go" and **इ** 2 P. with **अधि** 'to remember' substitute **गम्** in the Causal **इ** 2 P with **अधि** " to study" substitutes **गा** optionally in the Causal, Desiderative and in the third person of the Aorist

 Exception (3):— **आ** is necessarily substituted for the vowels of **क्री**—**इ**—**जि**—**मि**—**मी** to destroy-**दी-**and for those of **स्मि** if the effect is produced by the agent, **सिधू** if the import is not a spiritual topic, and **ली** 4 9. if it means 'to deceive, defeat or worship', **आ** is optionally substituted for the vowels of **चि** and **स्फुर्** and for those of **भी** if the effect is produced by the agent, and **वी** if it means to cause to conceive'

 (366) The penultimate **अ** is changed to its Vrıddhı substıtute before **अय**, as **खानय** from **खन्** 1 U, **छादय **from **छद्** 1. U.

 Exception (1):— Roots ending in **अम्** (except **कम्** 1 A.-**अम्** 1. P - **चम्** 1 P. - **शम्** 4 P. 'to see,' and **यम्** 1 P. when it does not mean to eat') and the following roots which are marked as **मिन्** in the Dhatupatha (Catalogue of Sanskrit verbs) do not change their vowel.

 **अक्-चक्** 1. P. 'to be satisfied,— and **स्तक्; काबू** 1. P **अगू**—**कम्**—**रगू**—**लग्**—**सम्**— **स्तग् **—**हग्** and **ह्लग् **(all 1 P );—**घटू** 1. A—**बट्** and **भटू** 1. P. in the sense of 'to speak'—and **नट्** 1. P. 'to dance',—**गडू** 1 P. **लड्** 1. "to loll the tongue’, forms **लडयति,** in the sense of 'fondle' **लाडयति, हेड्** 1 P.

‘to surround' forms **हिडयति, हेड्** 1 A. 'to disgrace' forms **हेडयति; कण्-रण्-फण्** (1. P. 'to go')**—** **चण्-शणू**—**अणू** (1. P. ' to give')—**व्यथ**—**प्रथ्** (1. A.),—**श्रथ्**—**क्नथू-क्रथ-क्लथ्** (1. P. to kill),—**म्रद्** 1. A., **स्खद्** 1. A, 'to discomfit **'**—**छद्** 10 U. 'to live, to be strong ' —and **मद्** 4 P. 'to rejoice, to be poor' all these form the Causal as **स्खदयति**—**छदयति**—**मदयति** in the limited senses noted here Otherwise they form **छादयति**—**मादयति स्खद्** with **अब** or **परि** forms as **अवस्खादयति, परिस्खादयति, चन** 1 P. ' to kill '-**वन्** with a preposition-**ध्वन्** 1 P to sound, —**स्त्रन्** 1 P. ' to deck' and **जन्** 4 A, **क्रप्** 1A. 'to pity,' **रम्** 1 A **क्रम्**—**गम्** (1 P.),—**त्वर्** 1 A.—**ज्वर्** 1. P. —**ज्वलू** —**ह्वल्**—**ह्मल्** when with prepositions and **चल्** meaning 'to quake' retain their vowels; otherwise these lengthen their vowels,—**दक्ष् **1 A 'to go or kill,' **प्रस्** 1 A 'to spread' and **क्नस्** 'to be crooked or to shine.'  
 Exception (2).—The roots **वन्**—**वम्**—**नम्**—**ज्वल्**—**ह्वल**—**ह्मल्**—**ध्वन्** and **चल्** lengthen their **अ** optionally when not preceded by a preposition.

 (367) The roots **रभ्**—**लम्**—**जम्** (1 A) and **रध्** 4 P. insert a nasal before their final, as **लम्भयति-ते.**

** **The root **हन्** forms its Causal **घातयति-ते** and **शद्** if the meaning be not to go' forms **शातयति-ते,** 'he causes to fall' **शादयात-ते** 'he causes to go'

 (368) Penultimate short vowel takes Guna substitute before **अय**, as **तेपय** from **तिप्** 1 A, **तोदय** from **तुद्** 6. U, **तर्षय** from **तृष्** 4. P and **कल्पय** from **क्लृप** 1 A.

 Exceptions—**स्फुर** 6. P substitutes **आ** optionally, **मृज् **takes Vriddhı, **गुह्** and **दुष्** 4 P lengthen their **उ** and **सिध्** substitutes **आ** in the Causal if the import be not a spiritual topic, as **साधयति** 'he accomplishes or prepares,' **सेधयति** ' he makes perfect' as used of sacred rites only.

 (369) **स्फाय्** 1. A. changes its **य्** to **व्** in the Causal, and **भ्रस्ज्** assumes two forms **भर्ज् **and **भ्रज्ज्.**

The root **रूह्** optionally substitutes **प्‌** for **न्** in the Causal,

 (370) Observe 195 (1—7) regarding **गुप्, धूप्,** &c and **अज** 1. P. ‘to go.’

 (371) Causal bases are generally conjugated in both the Padas.

 Exception (1):—The Causals of roots having the sense of ‘to swallow or to move’ and of the followmeg roots are conjugated in the Parasmaipada only—**ईष्ये**—**गर्ब**—**ज्वर्**—**नन्द्**—**लल्** (all 1. P );
**क्लिद्** 1. U; **गल्भ्**—**जन्**—**जभ्**—**रम्‌** and **व्यथ्‌** (all 1 A), **आस**— **इ ** with **अधि** ‘to study’(2 A ), **क्षु** and **रूद्** (2 P. ); **क्रुध-क्षुध् ** and **नश्**(all 4. P.),**खिद्—युध्—बुध्** and **युज् **(all 4 A) **क्लम्—ष्ठिव्** and **भ्रम् **(all 1. 4 7 ); **विज्** 6.7. A **लज्** and **लस्ज्** (6 A )

The following roots have the sense of ‘to swallow or to move ? :—

**क्षर**—**खाद्**—**खेल्**—**गल्**—**चम्‌**—**चल्‌**—**दु**—**स्नु**—**वेल्‌**—**वेप्‌** (all l P,) **कम्प्**—**ग्रस्‌**—**चेष्ट्**—**प्र** (1 A ), **धु** 5 U**, जक्ष् **and** प्सा** (2 P.), **लिह् 2** U**; गॄ** 6. 2, **तृण्‌** 8.U . and **अश्** 9. P

 Exception (2)—The Causals of **दम्** and **नृत्‌** (4, P)—**यस्** 1 4, P. with **आ**—**धे**—**पा-**-and **वस्** (1. P. )--**रुच्‌** 1 A and **वद्‌** with **अभि** are conjugated in the Atmanepada.
